Over the time however the simplicity of the game made it very popular with the kids age 5-10 years old. The game is played all over the world. It is known in Germany as Schwarzer Peter, in Sweden as Svarte Petter and in Finland as Musta Pekka (all meaning \"black Peter\") and in France as le pouilleux (\"the lousy/louse-ridden one\") or vieux garçon (\"old boy\").
